OBJECT Report 11012931 Debrief Check List (4PS Mob.)
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00;

  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Debrief Check List (4PS Mobile);
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  IF (StartDate = 0D) OR (EndDate = 0D) THEN
                    ERROR(Text005);
                  IF EndDate < StartDate THEN
                    ERROR(Text004);
                  IF NOT
                    (PrintContactInformation OR PrintObjects OR PrintSpecifications OR PrintDebriefText OR
                     PrintFollowUpJob OR PrintNotFinished OR PrintAdviceOrder)
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text001);

                  StartDateDec := DatetimeMgtCU.Datetime(StartDate,0T);
                  EndDateDec := DatetimeMgtCU.Datetime(EndDate+1,0T) - 0.0000000001;

                  GetRefPointNos();
                  SearchForServiceOrders();
                END;

  }

                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  FieldNo@1100525000 : Integer;
                                  RecRef@1100525001 : RecordRef;
                                  FldRef@1100525002 : FieldRef;
                                BEGIN
                                  // dp00563
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.FINDSET
                                  ELSE
                                    TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.NEXT;

                                  EVALUATE(FieldNo, TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type");
                                  RecRef.GETTABLE(ServiceOrder);
                                  FldRef := RecRef.FIELD(FieldNo);
                                  FldCaption := FldRef.CAPTION;
                                  CASE FieldNo OF
                                    ServiceOrder.FIELDNO("Phone No.") :
                                      BEGIN
                                        OldValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No.";
                                        NewValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No.";
                                      END;
                                    ServiceOrder.FIELDNO("Phone No. 2") :
                                      BEGIN
                                        OldValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No. 2";
                                        NewValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No. 2";
                                      END;
                                    ServiceOrder.FIELDNO("Mobile Phone No.") :
                                      BEGIN
                                        OldValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Mobile Phone No.";
                                        NewValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Mobile Phone No.";
                                      END;
                                    ServiceOrder.FIELDNO("Contact Name") :
                                      BEGIN
                                        OldValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Contact Name";
                                        NewValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Contact Name";
                                      END;
                                    ServiceOrder.FIELDNO("E-Mail") :
                                      BEGIN
                                        OldValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old E-Mail";
                                        NewValue := TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."E-Mail";
                                      END;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

                                BEGIN
                                  // DP00826
                                  ActionText := '';
                                  IF "Debrief Serv. Ord. Obj. (Mob.)"."Has Been Added by User" THEN
                                    ActionText += ', ' + Text006;
                                  IF "Debrief Serv. Ord. Obj. (Mob.)"."Has Been Created by User" THEN
                                    ActionText += ', ' + Text007;
                                  IF "Debrief Serv. Ord. Obj. (Mob.)"."Has Been Deleted by User" THEN
                                    ActionText += ', ' + Text008;
                                  IF "Debrief Serv. Ord. Obj. (Mob.)"."Has Been Modified by User" THEN
                                    ActionText += ', ' + Text009;
                                  IF "Debrief Serv. Ord. Obj. (Mob.)"."Has Been Replaced by User" THEN
                                    ActionText += ', ' + Text010;

                                  ActionText := COPYSTR(ActionText, 3);

                                  IF "Has Been Created by User" THEN BEGIN
                                    MobileDecentralObject.SETRANGE("Work Order No.", "Work Order No.");
                                    MobileDecentralObject.SETRANGE("Resource No. (Employee)", "Resource No. (Employee)");
                                    MobileDecentralObject.SETRANGE("Mobile Service Object No.", "Mobile Service Object No.");
                                    IF MobileDecentralObject.FINDFIRST THEN
                                      "Service Object No." := MobileDecentralObject."Service Object No.";
                                  END;

                                  ServiceObject.INIT;
                                  IF "Has Been Replaced by User" THEN
                                    IF NOT ServiceObject.GET("Service Object No.") THEN
                                      ServiceObject.INIT;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Work Order No.=FIELD(No.),
                            Resource No. (Employee)=FIELD(Resource No.) }

      Text003a@1100525024 : TextConst 'ENU=Technical Finished';
      Text003b@1100525023 : TextConst 'ENU=Ready';
      Text004@1100525022 : TextConst 'ENU=End Date may not be less than the Start Date.';

      NewValue@1100525029 : Text;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Service Order".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Service Order".TABLECAPTION, "Service Order".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetRefPointNos@1100525001();
    VAR
      lvRefPointRec@1100525000 : Record 11020271;
    BEGIN
      IF RefPointType IN [RefPointType::TechFinished, RefPointType::Both] THEN BEGIN
        lvRefPointRec.SETRANGE("Triggered by Field Service", '70');
        IF lvRefPointRec.FINDFIRST THEN
          RefPointTechFin := lvRefPointRec."No."
        ELSE
          ERROR(Text002, lvRefPointRec.FIELDCAPTION("Triggered by Field Service"), '70', Text003a, lvRefPointRec.TABLECAPTION);
      END;

      IF RefPointType IN [RefPointType::Ready, RefPointType::Both] THEN BEGIN
        lvRefPointRec.SETRANGE("Triggered by Field Service", '100');  //* Fixed code for 'Ready' in 4PS-Mobile.
        IF lvRefPointRec.FINDFIRST THEN
          RefPointReady := lvRefPointRec."No."
        ELSE
          ERROR(Text002, lvRefPointRec.FIELDCAPTION("Triggered by Field Service"), '100', Text003b, lvRefPointRec.TABLECAPTION);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchForServiceOrders@1100525005();
    VAR
      lvDocRefPointRec@1100525000 : Record 11020296;
      lvServOrderRec@1100525001 : Record 11012823;
      lvStartDate@1100528900 : DateTime;
      lvEndDate@1100528901 : DateTime;
      lvDate@1100528903 : Date;
      lvTime@1100528904 : Time;
      DateTimeMgt@1100528902 : Codeunit 11020218;
    BEGIN
      TmpServOrderRec.RESET;
      TmpServOrderRec.DELETEALL;

      lvDocRefPointRec.SETCURRENTKEY(Type, "Reference Point", "Date-Time (registrated)");
      lvDocRefPointRec.SETRANGE(Type, lvDocRefPointRec.Type::ServOrder);
      CASE RefPointType OF
        RefPointType::TechFinished: lvDocRefPointRec.SETRANGE("Reference Point", RefPointTechFin);
        RefPointType::Ready:   lvDocRefPointRec.SETRANGE("Reference Point", RefPointReady);
        RefPointType::Both:    lvDocRefPointRec.SETFILTER("Reference Point", '%1|%2', RefPointTechFin, RefPointReady);
        ELSE
          EXIT;
      END;
      //db.sn, 27-08-12
      lvDate := DateTimeMgt.Datetime2Date(StartDateDec);
      lvStartDate := CREATEDATETIME(lvDate, lvTime);
      lvDate := DateTimeMgt.Datetime2Date(EndDateDec);
      lvTime := 235959.999T;
      lvEndDate := CREATEDATETIME(lvDate, lvTime);
      //db.en, 27-08-12
      lvDocRefPointRec.SETRANGE("Date-Time (registrated)", lvStartDate, lvEndDate);
      "Service Order".COPYFILTER("No.", lvDocRefPointRec."Document No.");
      IF lvDocRefPointRec.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        lvServOrderRec.COPYFILTERS("Service Order");
        REPEAT
          IF NOT TmpServOrderRec.GET(lvDocRefPointRec."Document No.") THEN BEGIN
            lvServOrderRec.SETRANGE("No.", lvDocRefPointRec."Document No.");
            IF lvServOrderRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF lvServOrderRec."Date/Time Export to FSA" <> 0DT THEN BEGIN
                TmpServOrderRec := lvServOrderRec;
                TmpServOrderRec.INSERT;
              END;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL lvDocRefPointRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillTempDebriefWorkOrderMobile@1100525004(ServiceOrderNo@1100525000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      WorkOrder@1100525001 : Record 11229279;
      DebriefWorkOrderMobile@1100525002 : Record 11012679;
      LineNo@1100525003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // dp00563
      TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.RESET;
      TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.DELETEALL;

      WorkOrder.SETCURRENTKEY("Source Company","Source Type","Source No.");
      WorkOrder.SETRANGE("Source Company", COMPANYNAME);
      WorkOrder.SETRANGE("Source Type", WorkOrder."Source Type"::ServiceOrder);
      WorkOrder.SETRANGE("Source No.", ServiceOrderNo);
      IF WorkOrder.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          DebriefWorkOrderMobile.SETRANGE("Work Order No.", WorkOrder."No.");
          DebriefWorkOrderMobile.SETRANGE("Resource No. (Employee)", WorkOrder."Resource No.");
          DebriefWorkOrderMobile.SETRANGE(Status, DebriefWorkOrderMobile.Status::Processed);
          IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No." <> DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No." THEN BEGIN
              LineNo += 1;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INIT;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Work Order No." := WorkOrder."No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Line No." := LineNo;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No." := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No." := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type" := FORMAT("Service Order".FIELDNO("Phone No."));
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INSERT;
            END;
            IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No. 2" <> DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No. 2" THEN BEGIN
              LineNo += 1;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INIT;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Work Order No." := WorkOrder."No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Line No." := LineNo;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No. 2" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Phone No. 2";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No. 2" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Phone No. 2";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type" := FORMAT("Service Order".FIELDNO("Phone No. 2"));
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INSERT;
            END;
            IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Mobile Phone No." <> DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Mobile Phone No." THEN BEGIN
              LineNo += 1;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INIT;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Work Order No." := WorkOrder."No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Line No." := LineNo;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Mobile Phone No." := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Mobile Phone No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Mobile Phone No." := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Mobile Phone No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type" := FORMAT("Service Order".FIELDNO("Mobile Phone No."));
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INSERT;
            END;
            IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Contact Name" <> DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Contact Name" THEN BEGIN
              LineNo += 1;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INIT;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Work Order No." := WorkOrder."No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Line No." := LineNo;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Contact Name" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Contact Name";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Contact Name" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old Contact Name";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type" := FORMAT("Service Order".FIELDNO("Contact Name"));
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INSERT;
            END;
            IF DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old E-Mail" <> DebriefWorkOrderMobile."E-Mail" THEN BEGIN
              LineNo += 1;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INIT;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Work Order No." := WorkOrder."No.";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Line No." := LineNo;
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."E-Mail" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."E-Mail";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old E-Mail" := DebriefWorkOrderMobile."Old E-Mail";
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile."Order Type" := FORMAT("Service Order".FIELDNO("E-Mail"));
              TempDebriefWorkOrderMobile.INSERT;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL WorkOrder.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
